4a8(mdo sde2): tu gzar te/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bla ma lta gus pa dang / phu dud
4b1(mdo sde2): chen po byed pas/ me tog dang / bdug pa dang / spos dang / 'phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / na bza' dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan/
4b2(mdo sde2): dang / ba dan dang / dar gyi lda ldi dang / rol mo'i sgra dang / sil snyen dang / pheg rdog dang / klu dbyangs dang / rin po che'i lda ldi dang mu tig gi 'phreng ba dang / klu'i me
4b3(mdo sde2): tog dang / mu tig gi dra ba mchog tu mdzes pa rnam pa sna tshogs dpag tu med/ grangs med pa dag bcom ldan 'das la phul nas/ bskor ba byas te/ phyogs gcig tu
4b4(mdo sde2): 'dug go/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug nas/ smon lam rnams btab pa/ lus rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyis/ sangs rgyas
4b5(mdo sde2): dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rab 'byams rgya mtsho thams cad dang / sa dang chu dang me dang rlung tham
4b6(mdo sde2): kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul rnams dang / gzugs su snang ba thams cad kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul rnams las/ rdul phra rab kyi rdul re re la yang lus kyi sprin rgya mtsho bgrang ba'i rgya mtsho
4b7(mdo sde2): thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa grangs med dpag tu med bsam gyis mi khyab mtshungs pa med gzhal du med/ brjod du med pa las yang dag par 'das pa dag dang / lus
4b8(mdo sde2): re re la yang lag pa rgya mtsho'i sprin phyogs kun gyi rgyun du mngon par phyogs pa dpag tu med grangs med pa dag byin gyis brlabs nas/ rdul phra rab kyi rdul gyi cha re re las kyang
5a1(mdo sde2): @mchod pa thams cad kyi sprin rgya mtsho phyogs kun gyi gzhi rgyas pa 'gengs pa/ ma 'dres pa rnams kyis sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems
5a2(mdo sde2): dpa' thams cad la mchod pa bya'o snyam pa 'di lta ste/ kun tu spyod pa'i lus rgya mtsho'i sprin ma 'dres pa dpag tu med/ grangs med bsam gyis mi khyab gzhal du med/
5a3(mdo sde2): tshad med/ dpag tu med pa dag gis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams kyis ji ltar de
5a4(mdo sde2): bzhin du rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog dang / 'od zer stug po dang / nyi ma dang / zla ba thams cad lta bu'i lus kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / rin po che
5a5(mdo sde2): thams cad kyi phreng ba dang / me tog gi rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi snang ba chen po'i snying po'i khang pa brtsegs pa/ rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang /
5a6(mdo sde2): phye ma dang shing ljon pa thams cad kyi mdzod rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / spos dang / gdug pa thams cad kyi gzugs kun tu ston pa rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / sgra
5a7(mdo sde2): thams cad sgrogs pa'i rol mo'i sgra rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / spos thams cad kyi shing ljon pa mtsho sprin rnams kyis/ nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin
5a8(mdo sde2): gyis brlabs nas/ de la sogs pa mchod pa thams cad kyi sprin rgya mtsho dpag tu med grangs med bsam gyis mi khyab/ gzhal du med/ tshad med brjod du
5b1(mdo sde2): med pa/ ma 'dres pa rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod pa/
5b2(mdo sde2): bya'o// yul thams cad du bkod pa rnam par snang bar byas pa'i snying po can gyi nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams kyis/ nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin/
5b3(mdo sde2): gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho'i sprin thams cad du bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ni mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// thams
5b4(mdo sde2): cad kun tu snang ba'i rin po che'i char 'bab pa bkod pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba 'bar ba dang ldan pa/ sangs
5b5(mdo sde2): rgyas la nges par 'gyur ba'i dbyangs kyi nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams/ dang / kun tu sgra 'grengs pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi dbyangs can nor bu'i rgyal
5b6(mdo sde2): po rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / kun nas sgo rin po che 'od zer gyis sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa snang bar byed pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor ma 'dres
5b7(mdo sde2): pa rnams su bkod pa thams cad snang ba kun tu ston pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / 'od 'phro sgron ma sangs rgyas kyi yul thams cad kyi rjes su
5b8(mdo sde2): 'jug pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams su/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzhal med khang snang
6a1(mdo sde2): pa kun tu ston pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po'i rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi rdul la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas
6a2(mdo sde2): kyi sku snang ba rnam par snang bar byed pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams kyis/ nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs
6a3(mdo sde2): rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho sprin thams cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// rin po che dang /
6a4(mdo sde2): spos dang / me tog sna tshogs thams cad kyi khang pa brtsegs pa ma 'dres pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po kha dog mtha' yas pa thams cad kyis rab
6a5(mdo sde2): tu rgyan pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che'i sgron ma dang / spos kyi 'od 'phro ba can gyi khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / mu tig thams cad
6a6(mdo sde2): kyis rnam par spras pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / me tog thams cad kyi ze ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che'i 'phreng ba mtha' yas pas legs par brgyan
6a7(mdo sde2): pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs nas/ phyogs bcu kun tu 'od zer snang ba'i snying po can/ bkod pa zam
6a8(mdo sde2): cad yang dag par 'du ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi rdul gyis rab tu brgyan pa bkod pa du ma kun tu ston pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya
6b1(mdo sde2): mtsho sprin rnams dang / bkod pa thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa kun tu rgyas par 'gengs pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sgo kun tu me tog gi rta babs
6b2(mdo sde2): dril bu'i dra ba dbyangs kyi rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis/ nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad
6b3(mdo sde2): la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// gser dang rin po che sna tshogs kyi tshong zong dang / 'phreng ba dang / rin po che'i mgul gdub kyi snying
6b4(mdo sde2): po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / me tog ltar snang ba sna tshogs kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / in+d+ra nI la dang / 'dzam bu chu bo'i
6b5(mdo sde2): gser gyi pad+ma sna tshogs kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu rin po che'i sgron me'i pad+ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu rin
6b6(mdo sde2): po che snang gsal rgyal mtshan gyi pad ma sna tshogs kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po ches brgyan pa pad+ma sna tshogs kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri
6b7(mdo sde2): rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / in+da rnyil mdzes khar 'bar ba'i 'od zer can gyi pad+ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / 'od zer 'bar ba zad mi shes pa'i
6b8(mdo sde2): gzi brjid dang ldan pa'i pad+ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che 'bar ba mchog dam pa thams cad byung ba'i pad+ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya
7a1(mdo sde2): mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che 'bar ba mchog dam pa thams cad 'byung ba'i pad+ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs
7a2(mdo sde2): rgyas kyi gsung sgra'i 'od zer dang ldan pa'i pad+ma'i snying pa can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/
7a3(mdo sde2): sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// spos dang / nor bu sna tshogs tham
7a4(mdo sde2): cad kyi shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / kun nas sgo lo ma las thal mo sbyar ba'i sprin 'byung ba'i spos kyi shing rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / shing ldan pa thams
7a5(mdo sde2): cad kyi gzugs mtha' yas pa bkod pa kun tu ston pa'i shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / me tog thams cad kyi sprin rab tu 'phyang ba'i sprin shing ljon pa lta bu
7a6(mdo sde2): rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bkod pa thams cad 'byung ba'i mdzod mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa'i shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che 'od 'phro ba thams cad
7a7(mdo sde2): kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par snang bar byed pa'i shing ldan pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus phyed tsan dan thams cad kyi phye mar kun tu ston pa'i shing
7a8(mdo sde2): ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / byang chub kyi snying po thams cad kyi bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i 'od can gyi shing ljon pa'i rin po che'i gos thams cad kyi mdzod
7b1(mdo sde2): nyi ma ltar snang bar byas pa dang ldan pa'i shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sgra dbyangs thams cad sgrog pa yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs kun tu btong ba'i shing ljon pa
7b2(mdo sde2): rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che kha dog mtha' yas pa'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / kun tu mngon par phyogs pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po
7b3(mdo sde2): snang bar byed pa'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rgyan bkod pa thams cad kyi rab tu brgyan pa'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams
7b4(mdo sde2): dang / rin po che sna tshogs 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma'i 'phreng ba'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / kun nas sgra rin po che'i shing ljon pa 'byung ba'i snying
7b5(mdo sde2): po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / spos dang / me tog dang / pad+ma thams cad kyi 'phreng ba rin po che'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnam
7b6(mdo sde2): dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gdan bkod pa kun tu ston pa'i nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bkod pa thams
7b7(mdo sde2): cad kyi 'phreng ba rab tu sbyangs pa'i rta babs stegs bus rab tu brgyan pa/ rin po che'i sprin gyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / gser gyi ze ba can
7b8(mdo sde2): gyi 'od zer snang ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi bla re rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab par snang ba'i 'od mtha' yas par bkod pa thams cad kyi rgyan
8a1(mdo sde2): gyi bla re rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis/ nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' gangs
8a2(mdo sde2): chen mtsho sprin rgya mtsho thams cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// nor bu rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi gdugs rgya mtsho rnams
8a3(mdo sde2): kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs la/ rin po che bcu'i 'od zer snang ba bkod pa'i me tog gi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / mu tig kha
8a4(mdo sde2): dog mtha' yas pa'i mdzod kyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi snying rje'i sgo'i sgra'i nor bu rgyal po'i gdugs rgya
8a5(mdo sde2): mtsho sprin rnams spen rnams dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'od 'phro ba'i 'phreng ba'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che'i rdul kun tu snang bas rab tu
8a6(mdo sde2): brgyan pa'i dril bu dra bas dpyangs pa'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu thams cad kyi sdong bu'i yal ga'i rgyan can gyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nyi ma rnam
8a7(mdo sde2): bar snang bar byed pa'i 'od 'phro ba'i nor bu'i rgyal po dang / spos dang / gdugs thams cad kyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / tsan+dan gyi phye ma'i mdzod kun tu
8a8(mdo sde2): rgyas par 'gongs pa'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul rgya chen po snang bar byed pa kun tu bkod pas rgyas par 'gengs pa'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin
8b1(mdo sde2): ma 'dres pa rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpya' rgya mtsho sprin thams cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o//
8b2(mdo sde2): rin po che thams cad snang ba'i dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi gzugs kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa
8b3(mdo sde2): rnams dang / me tog gi sprin snang bar byed pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa'i 'od kyi dkyil
8b4(mdo sde2): 'khor dang ldan pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad snang bar gtogs pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / kun tus sgo sangs
8b5(mdo sde2): rgyas kyi yul sgrogs pa rin po che'i yal ga'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bai DUr+ya dang / rin po che'i rigs dang / nor bu rin po che'i rigs
8b6(mdo sde2): dang / nor bu rgyal po thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sems can gyi gzugs mtha' yas pa dag/ sems kyi skad cig la
8b7(mdo sde2): kun tu ston pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi smon lam las byung ba/ yid du 'ong ba'i sgra rab tu 'byin pa dang ldan pa'i 'od
8b8(mdo sde2): kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du sems can 'dul ba'i dbyangs can nor bu'i rgyal po'i dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams
9a1(mdo sde2): kyis/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o//
9a2(mdo sde2): nor bu thams cad kyi mdzod kyi 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gzugs dang / sgra dang / dri dang / ro dang / reg bya'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams
9a3(mdo sde2): dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos sgrogs rgyas par 'gengs pa'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs
9a4(mdo sde2): rgyas kyi zhing bkod pa thams cad sdud par byed 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / me tog gi khang pa brtsegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po
9a5(mdo sde2): che thams cad kyi rdul gyi 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bskal pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa thams cad du sangs rgyas 'byung bas sems can yongs su smin
9a6(mdo sde2): par byed pa'i sgrogs pa can gyi 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che mi zad pa thams cad bstan pa dang / me tog thams cad kyi ze ba'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin
9a7(mdo sde2): rnams dang / khri stan bkod pa thams cad kun tu ston pa'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams
9a8(mdo sde2): cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba kha dog mtha' yas pa rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa rnams dang /
9b1(mdo sde2): kun tu 'od kyi nor bu'i rgyal po 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zhing rgya chen po bkod pa snang bar byed pa'i 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin
9b2(mdo sde2): rnams dang / spos thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bkod pa thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sprul pa'i
9b3(mdo sde2): 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi shing gi ze ba 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / gos thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / byang chub
9b4(mdo sde2): sems dpa' mtha' yas pa'i spyod pa dbyangs can nor bu'i rgyal po'i 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / mu tig gi sgron ma thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa rnams
9b5(mdo sde2): kyis sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' gangs chen mtsho'i sprin gyi rgya mtsho thams cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// spos
9b6(mdo sde2): dang / me tog sna tshogs thams cad kyi rgya mtsho sprin bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams dang / rin po che 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi pad+ma'i dra ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu rin po che
9b7(mdo sde2): kha dog mtha' yas pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog dang ldan pa'i mu tig gi mdzod rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che dang / spos
9b8(mdo sde2): dang / tsan+dan thams cad kyi phye ma rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu'i rgyal po yid du 'ong zhing sdug pa mdzes pa'i
10a1(mdo sde2): dbyangs can rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nyi ma'i 'od kyi nor bu'i tshogs kyi 'phreng ba rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / rin po che'i mdzod mtha'
10a2(mdo sde2): yas rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / thams cad kun tu bzang po'i lus ma 'dres pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' gangs chen mtsho'i sprin gyi rgya
10a3(mdo sde2): mtsho thams cad la bsti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// zhes de lta bu'i smon lam btab po// klu'i rgyal po de dag gis kyang bcom ldan 'das
10a4(mdo sde2): la lan gsum bskor ba byas te zhabs la phyag 'tshal ba dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas/ rang rang gi stan la 'khod do// de'i tshe stong gsum gyi stong chen klu'i
10a5(mdo sde2): bdag po chen po phyir mi ldog pa'i smon lam gyi stobs can g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po zhes bya ba de bzhin
10a6(mdo sde2): gshegs pa la mchod pa dang phyag bya ba dang / bsnyen bkur bya ba dang / chos mnyan pa'i phyir 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir 'ongs so// de nas klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas
10a7(mdo sde2): rgya mtsho sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la
10a8(mdo sde2): gtsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud de/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// gal te zhus nas zhu ba lung bstan
10b1(mdo sde2): pa'i slad du/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bdeg la skabs phye na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la bdag
10b2(mdo sde2): phyogs 'ga' zhig zhu'o// de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho'i sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil
10b3(mdo sde2): 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// klu'i bdag po ci dang ci 'dod pa dris shig dang / ngas dris pa de dang de'i lung bstan pas khyod kyis sems
10b4(mdo sde2): rangs par bya'o// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho'i sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdug/
10b5(mdo sde2): lta bu'i rgyal pos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na kla thams cad klu'i sdug bsngal thams cad rgyan chad par 'gyur/ bde ba thams cad dang ldan
10b6(mdo sde2): pa dang / rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir dus dus su char gyi rgyun 'bebs par 'gyur/ rtswa dang / shing gel ba dang / sman dang / nags tshal tham
10b7(mdo sde2): cad 'grub par 'gyur/ 'bru thams cad skye bar 'gyur/ gzungs thams cad yang dag par skye bar 'gyur/ gang gis 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams bde ba dang ldan
10b8(mdo sde2): bar 'gyur/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal
11a1(mdo sde2): po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// klu'i bdag po khyod sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs/
11a2(mdo sde2): pa la don 'di yongs su 'dri bar sems pa legs so legs so// klu'i bdag po de'i phyir legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zungs shig dang / ngas khyod la bshad do//
11a3(mdo sde2): klu'i bdag po chos gcig dang ldan na klu thams cad kyi sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun chad par 'gyur/ bde ba dang ldan par 'gyur ro// chos gcig po gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/
11a4(mdo sde2): byams pa'o// klu'i bdag po byams pa de la gnas pa'i lha dang mi rnams ni mes mi tshig/ mtshon gyis mi tshugs/ chus mi 'khyer/ dug gis mi tshugs/ pha
11a5(mdo sde2): rol gyi dmag tshogs kyis mi non/ bde bar gnyid kyis log par 'gyur/ bde bar sad par 'gyur/ rang gi bsod nams kyis yongs su bsrung bar 'gyur/ bsod/
11a6(mdo sde2): nams chen po'i gzi brjid kyis gzi can du 'gyur/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis mi brdzi bar 'gyur/ mdzes pa dang / mthong na dga' ba dang / 'gro ba tham
11a7(mdo sde2): cad du thags thogs med par 'gyur/ sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun chad par 'gyur/ rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ bde ba thams cad dang ldan pa dang / ma'i chos
11a8(mdo sde2): bla ma rtogs nas/ lus zhig pa'i 'og tu tshangs pa'i 'jig rten du skye bar 'gyur te/ klu'i bdag po lha dang mi'i byams pa la gnas pa rnams kyi phan yon ni 'di dag go//
11b1(mdo sde2): klu'i bdag po de bas na byams pa'i lus kyi las dang / byams pa'i ngag gi las dang / byams pa'i yid kyi las kyis gnas par bya'o// klu'i bdag po gzhan yang
11b2(mdo sde2): bde ba thams cad sbyin pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs brjod par bya ste/ der klu thams cad kyi klu'i sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun gcod par byed/ bde ba thams cad sbyin par byed de/
11b3(mdo sde2): 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir dus dus su char gyi rgyun 'bebs par byed/ rtsa dang / shing gel ba dang / sman dang / nags tshal dang / lo thog thams cad skye bar byed do// klu'i
11b4(mdo sde2): bdag po de la bde ba thams cad sbyin pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs de gang zhe na/ tad+ya thA/ d+ha ra Ni d+ha ra Ni/ ut+ta ra ti/ sam pra tiSh+Thi te/ bi dza ya bar+Na/ sad+ya pra ti dz+nyA sa ra ha/ dz+nyA
11b5(mdo sde2): na pa ti/ ud pa da ni bI nA ma ni/ a bi She tsa ni/ a bi bya hA ra/ shu b+ha ba ti/ a dzi ma tu/ e hi ku me bA la na/ bA ha ha ra kle shA na/ d+hu na pA ba ma/ sho d+ha ya marga na/
11b6(mdo sde2): ni rA hi ka d+harma te shud+d+ha/ lo ka bi ti ma ri rA dzA sa du kha/ sha ma na sarba bud+d+ha e ba lo ka na a d+hiSh+Thi te pradz+nyA dz+nyA na b+he swA hA/ klu'i bdag po gzungs kyi tshig don thams cad sgrub/
11b7(mdo sde2): par byed pa/ chos kyi sku la 'jugs/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ bde ba thams cad sbyin pa 'di dag bzung bar bya/ brjod par bya'o//
11b8(mdo sde2): klu'i bdag po gzhan yang sprin gyi rigs las byang ba'i byin gyis brlabs bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi snying po sprul par byed pa/ ye shes kyi tog gi chu'i rgyun gyi sprin gyi
12a1(mdo sde2): dkyil 'khor dpal dang ldan pa gser gyi 'od zer rnam par snang ba'i byed pa/ skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas gcig las byung ba'i rus dang rigs kyi de bzhin
12a2(mdo sde2): gshegs pa rnams kyi mtshan bzung bar bya/ yid la bya'o// de dag gis klu thams cad dang / klu'i rigs thams cad dang / klu'i rus thams cad dang / klu'i tshe rigs thams cad
12a3(mdo sde2): dang / klu 'byung ba thams cad dang / klu'i skye gnas thams cad dang / klu'i rgyal po thams cad dang / klu'i bu mo thams cad dang / klu'i g.yog thams cad kyi klu'i sdug bsngal zam
12a4(mdo sde2): cad rgyun gcod par byed/ bde ba'i yo byad sgrub par byed do// klu'i bdag po de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de dag gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
12a5(mdo sde2): rnam par snang mdzad snying po can gyi sprin chen po la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa klu'i rigs las byung ba sprin gyis rnam par mdzes la phyag 'tshal lo//
12a6(mdo sde2): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi chu 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dpal ldan sprin gyi gzi brjid la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom
12a7(mdo sde2): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen 'byung la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rlung gi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par 'joms pa'i sprin la
12a8(mdo sde2): phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa nam mkha' dpag med la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen po'i grog 'bar ba'i
12b1(mdo sde2): tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen mthu rtsal dpa' bo phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin mdzes la
12b2(mdo sde2): phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin sdug chen po la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi dkyil 'khor chen po la phyag
12b3(mdo sde2): 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi 'od la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen seng ge la phyag 'tshal lo// bco
12b4(mdo sde2): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen gdugs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa blta sdug sprin chen la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan
12b5(mdo sde2): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen pos khebs pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin las byung ba snang bar byed pa'i dkyil 'khor phyogs
12b6(mdo sde2): bcu mtho 'gebs rnga'i sgra dbyangs shin tu rab sgrogs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen bsil 'byung mi dga' rab 'joms sgra za//
12b7(mdo sde2): sgrog pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen 'dal la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa gang+gA'i chu sprin
12b8(mdo sde2): la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rtsal gyis sprin ltar dpa' bo la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'brug gi
13a1(mdo sde2): sgra bsgrags pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin kun tu ston la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'ad
13a2(mdo sde2): de bzhin gshegs pa sprin rgya chen la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin 'dzag la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
13a3(mdo sde2): gshegs pa sprin ltar rnam par sgrogs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin ltar 'phags la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan
13a4(mdo sde2): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin lta bu'i na bza' mnabs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyis lo tog bskyed la phyag
13a5(mdo sde2): 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi gnas la gnas pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tshor sprin gyi sprin
13a6(mdo sde2): la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin 'du bar mdzad pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin rnam par rgyas pa
13a7(mdo sde2): la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen ut+pal la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen spos kyi sku la phyag
13a8(mdo sde2): 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen 'phags la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo//
13b1(mdo sde2): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen 'od mdzad la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen byin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan
13b2(mdo sde2): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa nor bu rin po che chen po'i sprin lta bu la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin ltar rnam par 'joms pa la phyag 'tshalo//
13b3(mdo sde2): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi chu bo la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin sdud la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de
13b4(mdo sde2): bzhin gshegs pa dus ma yin pa'i sprin dang lce 'bab pa rnam par 'joms pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen po ltar nam mkha'i
13b5(mdo sde2): mthong nas bsgrags pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen sgra 'byin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin
13b6(mdo sde2): chen char chu skyes la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs bsnyems pa'i gzi brjid sgrub pa'i sprin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
13b7(mdo sde2): pa ro bro ba drug dang ldan pa'i chu chen po'i sprin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa chu 'thor sprin chen la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
13b8(mdo sde2): gshegs pa sprin chen rgya mtsho 'gengs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa char mi 'babs pa na sprin gyis kun tu 'gebs pa la phyag 'tshal lo//
14a1(mdo sde2): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gzugs mtha' yas la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa
14a2(mdo sde2): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas sprin chen po thams cad rnam par sgrub pa 'dzam bu'i sprin gyi dpal gyi gzi brjid 'od mdzad pa/ sprin gyi 'od zer can rnams la phyag 'tshalo//
14a3(mdo sde2): klu'i bdag po de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'di dag brjod pas/ klu thams cad kyi sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun chad pa dang / bde ba thams cad dang ldan pa dang / 'dzam
14a4(mdo sde2): bu'i gling 'dir dus dus su char pa'i rgyun 'bab pa dang / rtsa dang / shing gel ba dang / sman dang / nags tshal dang / lo tog thams cad bskyed par byed do// de nas
14a5(mdo sde2): bcom ldan 'das la stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho'i sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal pos gsol ba
14a6(mdo sde2): btab pa/ bcom ldan 'das slad ma'i tshe slad ma'i dus na 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char mi 'bab pa'i tshe/ gang dag brjod na tshar gyi rgyun chen po 'bab par bgyid pa dang / mi bzad
14a7(mdo sde2): pa'i dus kyi tshe dang / gnod pa 'byung ba'i dus kyi tshe dang / nad dang 'chi ba'i dus kyi tshe dang / skar ma ma rungs pa gnas pa'i dus kyi tshe dang / yams kyi nad dang / 'cheg
14a8(mdo sde2): dang / gnod pa thams cad rab tu zhi bar bgyid pa/ de lta bu'i gzungs kyi gsang sngag kyi gzhi rnams bshad du gsol// sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs kyis byin
14b1(mdo sde2): gyis brlab tu gsol// gang dag klu thams la bskul ma 'debs par 'gyur ba dang / lha thams cad rab tu dga' bar 'gyur ba dang / bdud thams cad rnam par
14b2(mdo sde2): 'joms par 'gyur ba dang / sems can thams cad rnam par 'joms par 'gyur ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi 'jigs pa thams cad 'jig par 'gyur ba dang /
14b3(mdo sde2): gnod pa thams cad bzlog par 'gyur ba dang / zhi ba dang bde legs su 'gyur ba bgyid pa dang / rgyu skar ma rungs pas bgyis pa rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ba dang / bcom
14b4(mdo sde2): ldan 'das kyis char pa'i bar chad lnga gsungs pa gang lags pa de dag thams cad sel bar 'gyur ba dang / 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char pa'i rgyun legs par 'bab par 'gyur
14b5(mdo sde2): ba de lta bu'i gzungs kyi gsang sngags kyi gzhi rnams bcom ldan 'das mchog tu thugs rje dang ldan dang / sems can thams cad la phan par thugs brtse ba ldan pas bshad
14b6(mdo sde2): du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba 'tshal lo// de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis klu'i rgyal po g.yog mtha' yas
14b7(mdo sde2): rgya mtsho'i sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// klu'i bdag po khyod sems can thams cad kyi don dang phan
14b8(mdo sde2): pa dang bde ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba 'debs pa legs so legs so// klu'i bdag po de'i phyir legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang /
15a1(mdo sde2): snying rje chen po las byung ba 'brug chen po'i sgra can bsgyings pa dpa' ba'i tog ces bya ba'i gzungs/ sems can thams cad kyi don dang /
15a2(mdo sde2): phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gsungs pa/ byin gyis brlabs pa rjes su yid rang ba bshad par bya ste/ de ni char med pa'i tshe char 'bab par byed/
15a3(mdo sde2): char ches na gcod/ 'chi ba'i gnod pa rab tu zhi bar byed/ klu thams cad bskul bar byed/ lha thams cad sim par byed/ bdud thams cad rnam par 'joms par byed/
15a4(mdo sde2): sems can thams cad bde ba thams cad dang ldan par byed do// tad+ya thA/ ma hA dz+nyA na/ a ba b+ha sa ni/ shri ti dzo yag smi dri ti ba kra ma badz+ra sad ha ta ni/ pha ra mi bi rA dza/ ni
15a5(mdo sde2): ra ma la ku ma ke tu sUr+ya pra b+he/ bi ma lAng ga yaSh+Ti/ b+ha ra b+ha ra/ saM b+ha ra saM b+ha ra/ du du ma bu/ ha na ha na/ ma hA pra b+he/ bi d+hu'u ta ma hA mo hA an d+ha ku re/ pradz+nyA gra shud+d+he/ pa ri/
15a6(mdo sde2): bu bu ra Na me tra/ me tra bI ra Na srAn+d+ha/ me d+ha ma bud+d+ha re/ dza la dza la/ dza la mA bud+d+ha re/ sho d+h+ya dag ku su me/ da sha ba le/ tsa tA ra pe shwa ra te/ ASh+ma da sha a bi ni ga bud+d+ha d+harme/ shu
15a7(mdo sde2): ba ma ti/ puN+ye ra hi/ shuk+Sha d+ha ra ma sa ma nI ti/ gam+b+hI re bi ra dza sde/ bi ma le/ bi she Sha pra ba te/ na ra swa ba d+hame/ sarba lo ka N+yaiSh+Tha/ dz+yeSh+Tha pa ra pra ba re/ a nud ta re/ a sang ge/
15a8(mdo sde2): d+ha ra d+ha ra/ d+hi ri d+hi ri/ d+hu ru d+hu ru/ shan ta ma te/ shan ta ba be/ tsa tsa ra/ tsa ra tsa ra/ tsi ri tsi ra/ tsu ru tsu ru/ ba ra ma bud+d+hA nu ma te/ ma hA pradz+nyA pa ra mi te swA hA/ de bzhin
15b1(mdo sde2): gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad ye shes rgya mtsho dang ldan pa la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas 'dzam bu/
15b2(mdo sde2): gling 'dir char 'babs pa'i phyir klu thams cad kyi snying po brjod par bya'o// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis bden pas char pa'i bar chad byed pa lnga
15b3(mdo sde2): stsal bar bya'o// sad+ya the dan/ sa ra sa ra/ si ri si ri/ su ru su ru/ ne ga nan/ dzi bi dzi bi/ dzu bu dzu bu/ klu chen po dag tshur gshegs/ sangs rgyas kyi bden pas/
15b4(mdo sde2): 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char rab tu phob cig/ tsa ra tsa ra/ tsi ri tsi ri/ tsu ru tsu ru/ klu'i bdag po chen po dag tshur gshegs/ kyai klu chen po dag sangs rgyas kyi bden pas 'dzam bu
15b5(mdo sde2): gling 'dir char rab tu phob cig/ ba ra ba ra/ bi ri bi ri/ bu ru bu ru/ sangs rgyas kyi bden pas/ klu thams cad dgug par bya'o// byams pa'i sems dang Na snying rje'i
15b6(mdo sde2): sems dang / dga' ba'i sems dang / btang snyoms kyi sems dang / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs dang / bden pa dang /
15b7(mdo sde2): bsam pa chen pos klu'i bdag po tshur gshegs sangs rgyas rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan rnams dran par gyis shig
15b8(mdo sde2): b+ha ra b+ha ra/ b+hi ri b+hi ri/ b+hu ru b+hu ru/ chu chen po'i chu dang / sprin gyi chu 'chad pa can lag gis 'gro chen po'i g.yog rnams byams pa'i sems kyis tshur gshegs/ ston gyi/
16a1(mdo sde2): bstan pa dam pa dran par bgyis/ g+ha Na g+ha Da/ g+hi Di g+hi Di/ g+hu Du g+hu Ta/ drag shul can khro ba shugs chen po dang ldan pa/ dug chen
16a2(mdo sde2): 1po'i lce 'byin pa rnams byams pa'i sems dang ldan par tshur gshegs/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bden pas 'dzam bu gling 'dir char phob cig swA hA/ ta
16a3(mdo sde2): Ta ta Ta tai Ti ti Ti/ tu Ta tu Tu/ nor bu chen po'i cod pan thogs pa dang ldan pa/ sbrul gdug pa'i gzugs can rnams/ dkon mchog gsum gyi byin gyis brlab
16a4(mdo sde2): dran par gyis la/ rdo rje 'chang gi bden pas 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char phob cig swA hA/ ka la ka la/ ki li ki li/ ku lu ku lu/ chu chen po la gnas pa dang ldan pa/ sprin
16a5(mdo sde2): chen po brtsegs pa'i gzhon pa la zhon nas mngon par 'gro ba rnams tshur gshegs/ byams pa'i sems kyis 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char gyi rgyun phob cig/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
16a6(mdo sde2): bden pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin rlabs kyis/ lag na rdo rjes bsgo ba/ ra la ra la/ ri li ri li/ ru lu ru lu/ lag gis 'gro ba thams cad khyed rnams nyid med par
